{"type":"item.completed","item":{"id":"item_1","type":"command_execution","command":"/bin/zsh -lc \"sed -n '1,240p' docs/design-docs/clo-374-per-step-sandbox-routing.md\"","aggregated_output":"# CLO-374 Design: Per-step sandbox routing for Codex and Gemini backends (FR-21)\n\n**Author:** CLO-374 orchestrator (pi)\n**Date:** 2026-05-18\n**Source PRD:** `docs/prds/prd-phase-2-predictable-cli-execution-v5.md` §FR-21, §9 release plan step 8\n**Discovery report:** `docs/discovery/clo-374.md`\n\n---\n\n## 1. Problem\n\nCodex sandbox mode (`-s read-only | workspace-write | danger-full-access`) and Gemini's `--approval-mode` are currently hardcoded into each backend's argv builder. The `StepContext.sandbox` field exists (from CLO-371) but is never populated. Without per-step sandbox:\n\n- `apply_edits` steps cannot use Codex because `-s read-only` blocks file writes\n- Gemini has no `--approval-mode` support at all\n- Users cannot control sandbox granularity per step\n\n**Out of scope:**\n- FR-22 (default `workspace-write` for `apply_edits` steps with no explicit sandbox) — separate CLO\n- FR-23 (per-step timeout) — already handled by `step.timeout` field\n- FR-24/24a (per-step options, `include_directories`) — separate CLOs\n- Claude/Ollama/Bedrock sandbox support — no-op, sandbox is meaningful only for CLI subprocess backends\n\n---\n\n## 2. Design\n\n### 2.1 `Step` struct — add `sandbox` field\n\n**File:** `src/workflow.rs`\n\nAdd to the `Step` struct:\n\n```rust\n/// Sandbox mode for subprocess backends (FR-21).\n/// Controls Codex `-s` and Gemini `--approval-mode`.\n/// None = backend default (read-only).\n#[serde(default)]\npub sandbox: Option<SandboxMode>,\n```\n\n**Import:** Add `use crate::backend::SandboxMode;` to the imports in `src/workflow.rs`.\n\n**Deserialization:** `SandboxMode` is defined in `src/backend/context.rs`. It needs `serde::Deserialize` and `serde::Serialize` derives with `#[serde(rename_all = \"kebab-case\")]` to parse `read-only`, `workspace-write`, `danger-full-access` from YAML. The file already imports serde types via `use serde_json::Value` but does not have `use serde::Deserialize;` — add `use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};`.\n\n**Current `SandboxMode` has no serde derives.** We need to add them:\n\n```rust\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Deserialize, Serialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = \"kebab-case\")]\npub enum SandboxMode {\n    ReadOnly,\n    WorkspaceWrite,\n    DangerFullAccess,\n}\n```\n\n### 2.2 `step_context()` — thread sandbox\n\n**File:** `src/workflow.rs` (line ~167)\n\n```rust\nfn step_context<'a>(\n    step: &'a Step,\n    workflow: &Workflow,\n    prompt: &'a str,\n    cwd: &'a Path,\n) -> backend::StepContext<'a> {\n    backend::StepContext {\n        sandbox: step.sandbox,\n        timeout: workflow\n            .step_timeout(step)\n            .map(std::time::Duration::from_millis),\n        ..backend::StepContext::from_prompt(prompt, cwd, step.model.as_deref())\n    }\n}\n```\n\nUpdate the doc comment to remove \"sandbox remains empty\" note.\n\n### 2.3 `CodexBackend` — dynamic sandbox arg injection\n\n**File:** `src/backend/codex.rs`\n\n**Change the `query` method** to build args dynamically based on `ctx.sandbox` instead of using `self.args` verbatim.\n\nKey logic:\n\n```rust\nasync fn query(&self, ctx: StepContext<'_>) -> Result<QueryOutput, BackendError> {\n    // ... existing setup ...\n\n    let mut cmd = Command::new(&self.command);\n\n    // Base args from config (may be empty -> use recommended defaults)\n    if self.args.is_empty() {\n        cmd.args([\"exec\", \"--json\", \"--ephemeral\"]);\n    } else {\n        cmd.args(&self.args);\n    }\n\n    // Sandbox flag: ctx.sandbox overrides, fallback to read-only\n    let sandbox = ctx.sandbox.unwrap_or(SandboxMode::ReadOnly);\n    let sandbox_str = match sandbox {\n        SandboxMode::ReadOnly => \"read-only\",\n        SandboxMode::WorkspaceWrite => \"workspace-write\",\n        SandboxMode::DangerFullAccess => \"danger-full-access\",\n    };\n    cmd.arg(\"-s\").arg(sandbox_str);\n\n    // Model override\n    if let Some(m) = effective_model.as_ref() {\n        cmd.arg(\"--model\").arg(m);\n    }\n\n    // Prompt as positional arg\n    cmd.arg(\"--\").arg(prompt)\n        .current_dir(cwd)\n        // ... rest unchanged ...\n}\n```\n\n**Design decisions:**\n- Sandbox is injected AFTER base args so it overrides any `-s` in custom config args. This is intentional — per-step sandbox should take priority over backend config.\n- `--ephemeral` is included ONLY in the no-custom-args default set. If the user configured custom args, we do NOT inject `--ephemeral` (preserving their explicit config).\n- When custom `config.args` are provided, we still append sandbox at the end, preserving user-configured flags like `--ignore-user-config`.\n\n### 2.4 `GeminiBackend` — dynamic approval-mode injection\n\n**File:** `src/backend/gemini.rs`\n\nIn the shell command string construction, append `--approval-mode <mode>` based on `ctx.sandbox`:\n\n```rust\nlet approval_flag = match ctx.sandbox {\n    Some(SandboxMode::ReadOnly) => \" --approval-mode plan\",\n    Some(SandboxMode::WorkspaceWrite) => \" --approval-mode auto_edit\",\n    Some(SandboxMode::DangerFullAccess) => \" --approval-mode yolo\",\n    None => \"\",  // backend default (no restriction)\n};\n```\n\n**Gemini approval mode mapping** (verified against `gemini-cli-gap-analysis.md` §5.8; final verification against `gemini --help` required at implementation time):\n\n| SandboxMode | `--approval-mode` | Effect |\n|---|---|---|\n| `ReadOnly` | `plan` | Read-only, no mutations |\n| `WorkspaceWrite` | `auto_edit` | Auto-approve edit tools |\n| `DangerFullAccess` | `yolo` | Auto-approve all (CLI only) |\n| `None` | (not added) | Gemini default behaviour |\n\n**Design decision:** When `ctx.sandbox` is `None` (no per-step override), we add no `--approval-mode` flag. This differs from Codex where `None` falls back to `read-only`. Rationale: Gemini backends may be used for read-only tasks today without any flag; adding `--approval-mode plan` would be a behavioural change for all existing Gemini configurations. The v5 PRD treats `None` as \"backend default\" which for Gemini means the installed default (typically interactive).\n\n### 2.5 `SandboxMode` — add serde derives\n\n**File:** `src/backend/context.rs`\n\n```rust\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Deserialize, Serialize)]\n#[serde(rename_all = \"kebab-case\")]\npub enum SandboxMode {\n    ReadOnly,\n    WorkspaceWrite,\n    DangerFullAccess,\n}\n```\n\nAlso update the `#[allow(dead_code)]` annotation — remove it once `Step.sandbox` starts consuming the enum.\n\n### 2.6 Other backends — no-op\n\nClaude, Ollama, and Bedrock backends do not use sandbox/approval-mode CLIs. No changes needed. The `ctx.sandbox` field is silently ignored.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Implementation plan\n\n### 3.1 Files to change\n\n| File | Change | Lines |\n|---|---|---|\n| `src/backend/context.rs` | Add serde derives to `SandboxMode` | ~3 lines |\n| `src/workflow.rs` | Add `sandbox` field to `Step` struct | ~5 lines |\n| `src/workflow.rs` | Thread `sandbox` in `step_context()` | ~2 lines + comment update |\n| `src/workflow.rs` | Remove \"sandbox remains empty\" doc comment | ~1 line |\n| `src/backend/codex.rs` | Dynamic sandbox arg injection in `query()` | ~15 lines |\n| `src/backend/gemini.rs` | Dynamic approval-mode in shell command | ~10 lines |\n| `src/backend/mod.rs` | Re-export `SandboxMode` (already done) | 0 lines |\n\n### 3.2 Test plan\n\n**Type: Unit tests for arg building**\n\nSince we cannot easily capture process argv from a real `Command`, use a test helper `MockBackend` (or a test-only struct with the same arg-building logic) that captures the intended argv as a `Vec<String>`.\n\n| Test | Assertion |\n|---|---|\n| `codex_sandbox_default` | `None` → Codex argv contains `-s read-only` |\n| `codex_sandbox_workspace_write` | `Some(WorkspaceWrite)` → Codex argv contains `-s workspace-write` |\n| `codex_sandbox_danger_full_access` | `Some(DangerFullAccess)` → Codex argv contains `-s danger-full-access` |\n| `codex_defaults_include_ephemeral` | Default args include `--ephemeral` |\n| `gemini_sandbox_default` | `None` → Gemini argv does NOT contain `--approval-mode` |\n| `gemini_sandbox_read_only` | `Some(ReadOnly)` → Gemini argv contains `--approval-mode plan` |\n| `gemini_sandbox_workspace_write` | `Some(WorkspaceWrite)` → Gemini argv contains `--approval-mode auto_edit` |\n| `gemini_sandbox_danger` | `Some(DangerFullAccess)` → Gemini argv contains `--approval-mode yolo` |\n| `step_yaml_parsing` | `sandbox: workspace-write` → `Step.sandbox == Some(WorkspaceWrite)` |\n| `step_yaml_default` | No `sandbox` field → `Step.sandbox == None` |\n\n### 3.3 Risk assessment\n\n| Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| Gemini approval-mode names differ from gap analysis | Medium | Low | Verify with `gemini --help` at implementation time |\n| Codex custom config args contain `-s` already | Low | Medium | Sandbox is appended after base args; per-step wins over config |\n| Shell command string escaping breaks for Gemini | Low | Medium | The existing Gemini shell-cmd pattern already handles single-quote escaping; approval-mode is a simple append |\n| `--ephemeral` breaks existing Codex behaviour | Low | Low | Per codex-quick-ref.md, this is a recommended addition; it only suppresses session artifact persistence |\n\n---\n\n## 4. Acceptance criteria\n\n- [ ] `SandboxMode` has serde derives with `rename_all = \"kebab-case\"` parsing `read-only`, `workspace-write`, `danger-full-access`\n- [ ] `Step` struct has `sandbox: Option<SandboxMode>` field with `#[serde(rename = \"sandbox\")]`\n- [ ] `step_context()` in `src/workflow.rs` threads `step.sandbox` into `StepContext.sandbox`\n- [ ] `CodexBackend::query` uses `ctx.sandbox` to inject `-s <mode>`; `None` → `read-only`\n- [ ] `GeminiBackend::query` uses `ctx.sandbox` to inject `--approval-mode <mode>`; `None` → no flag\n- [ ] Default Codex args include `--ephemeral` (per codex-quick-ref.md recommended defaults)\n- [ ] `cargo test` passes with argv-capture tests for all sandbox levels\n- [ ] `cargo clippy -- -D warnings` clean\n- [ ] Gemini approval-mode names verified against `gemini --help` and documented in PR description\n\n---\n\n## 5. Prior decisions consulted\n\n- **ADR: Backend trait interface** — not modified, interface already supports `StepContext`\n- **CLO-371 design** (`docs/designs/clo-371-migrate-backendquery-to-stepcontext.md`) — established `StepContext.sandbox` field; this CLO wires it end-to-end\n- **System patterns** (`docs/context/system-patterns.md`) — per-step config threads through `step_context()` bridge function; this CLO follows the same pattern as `model` and `timeout`\n- **Codex quick-ref** (`docs/investigations/codex-quick-ref.md`) — recommended default args include `--ephemeral`, sandbox flags documented\n- **Gemini gap analysis** (`docs/investigations/gemini-cli-gap-analysis.md`) — approval-mode names: `plan`, `auto_edit`, `yolo`\n","exit_code":0,"status":"completed"}}

Workflow engine - declarative multi-step LLM pipelines\n//!\n//! Workflows are TOML files that define a sequence of steps, each using\n//! a backend to process a prompt. Steps can depend on previous steps\n//! and interpolate their outputs.\n//!\n//! Agentic features:\n//! - `shell` steps run shell commands instead of LLM queries\n//! - `apply_edits` parses JSON edits from LLM output and applies them\n//! - `verify` runs a shell command after for workflow execution\n#[derive(Debug, Error)]\npub enum WorkflowError {\n    #[error(\"Workflow '{workflow}': step '{step}' depends on unknown step '{missing}'\\n  hint: check depends_on list\")]\n    MissingDependency {\n        workflow: String,\n        step: String,\n        missing: String,\n    },\n\n    #[error(\n        \"Workflow '{workflow}': circular dependency detected: {chain}\\n  hint: remove the cycle\"\n    )]\n    CircularDependency { workflow: String, chain: String },\n\n    #[error(\"Workflow '{workflow}': step '{step}' has unknown variable '{{{{ {variable} }}}}'\\n  hint: valid forms are steps.X.output, steps.X.field, env.VAR, arg.N, workflow.backends\")]\n    UnknownVariable {\n        workflow: String,\n        step: String,\n        variable: String,\n    },\n\n    #[error(\"Workflow '{workflow}': duplicate step names: {}\\n  hint: each step must have a unique name\", duplicates.join(\", \"))]\n    DuplicateStepNames {\n        workflow: String,\n        duplicates: Vec<String>,\n    },\n\n    #[error(\"Workflow '{workflow}': step '{step}' has min_deps_success but no dependencies\\n  hint: min_deps_success requires depends_on to be non-empty\")]\n ({actual_deps})\\n  hint: reduce min_deps_success or add more dependencies\")]\n    MinDepsSuccessExceedsDeps {\n        workflow: String,\n        step: String,\n        min_deps_success: usize,\n        actual_deps: usize,\n    },\n\n    #[error(\"Workflow '{workflow}': step '{step}' has timeout ({timeout}ms) below minimum ({min}ms)\\n  hint: use 0 for no timeout, or a value >= {min}ms\")]\n    TimeoutTooSmall {\n        workflow: String,\n        step: String,\n        timeout: u64,\n        min: u64,\n    },\n}\nuse futures::future::join_all;\nuse serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};\nuse std::collections::HashMap;\nuse std::path::{Path, PathBuf};\nuse std::sync::LazyLock;\nuse tokio::process::Command;\n\n/// Default timeout for workflow steps in milliseconds (2 minutes)\nconst DEFAULT_STEP_TIMEOUT_MS: u64 = 120_000;\n\n/// Minimum timeout value in milliseconds (values 1 to MIN-1 are rejected)\nconst MIN_TIMEOUT_MS: u64 = 100;\n\n/// Default verify output cap: 1 MiB per stream. pub new: String,\n}\n\n/// A workflow definition loaded from TOML\n#[derive(Debug, Deserialize, Serialize, Clone)]\npub struct Workflow {\n    pub name: String,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub description: Option<String>,\n    /// Extend another workflow by name (inherits steps, can override by name)\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub extends: Option<String>,\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub steps: Vec<Step>,\n    /// Default continue_on_error for all steps (steps can override)\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub continue_on_error: bool,\n    /// Default timeout for all steps in milliseconds (steps can override)\n    #[serde(default)]\n    pub timeout: Option<u64>,\n}\n\nimpl Workflow {\n    /// Validate workflow configuration at load time\n    pub fn validate(&self) -> Result<(), WorkflowError> {\n        for step in &self.steps {\n            if let Some(min) = step.min_deps_success {\n                let deps_count = step.depends_on.len();\n                if min > deps_count {\n                    return Err(WorkflowError::MinDepsSuccessExceedsDeps {\n                        workflow: self.name.clone(),\n                        step: step.name.clone(),\n                        min_deps_success: min,\n                        actual_deps: deps_count,\n                    });\n                }\n            }\n            // Validate timeout: 0 means no timeout, but values between 1 and MIN are likely mistakes\n            let effective_timeout = self.step_timeout(step);\n            if let Some(timeout) = effective_timeout {\n                if timeout > 0 && timeout < MIN_TIMEOUT_MS {\n                    return Err(WorkflowError::TimeoutTooSmall {\n                        workflow: self.name.clone(),\n                        step: step.name.clone(),\n                        timeout,\n                        min: MIN_TIMEOUT_MS,\n                    });\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        Ok(())\n    }\n\n    /// Get the effective continue_on_error for a step (step-level overrides workflow-level)\n    pub fn step_continue_on_error(&self, step: &Step) -> bool {\n        step.continue_on_error.unwrap_or(self.continue_on_error)\n    }\n\n    /// Get the effective timeout for a step (step-level overrides workflow-level)\n    pub fn step_timeout(&self, step: &Step) -> Option<u64> {\n        step.timeout.or(self.timeout)\n    }\n}\n\n/// Build a `StepContext` from a `Step` and current workflow defaults.\n///\n/// History/schema/options remain empty until their Problem\\n\\nCodex sandbox mode (`-s read-only | workspace-write | danger-full-access`) and Gemini's `--approval-mode` are currently hardcoded into each backend's argv builder. The `StepContext.sandbox` field exists (from CLO-371) but is never populated. Without per-step sandbox:\\n\\n- `apply_edits` steps cannot use Codex because `-s read-only` blocks file writes\\n- Gemini has no `--approval-mode` support at all\\n- Users cannot control sandbox granularity per step\\n\\n**Out of scope:**\\n- FR-22 (default `workspace-write` for `apply_edits` steps with no explicit sandbox) — separate CLO\\n- FR-23 (per-step timeout) — already handled by `step.timeout` field\\n- FR-24/24a (per-step options, `include_directories`) — separate CLOs\\n- Claude/Ollama/Bedrock sandbox support — no-op, sandbox is meaningful only for CLI subprocess backends\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 2. Design\\n\\n### 2.1 `Step` struct — add `sandbox` field\\n\\n**File:** `src/workflow.rs`\\n\\nAdd to the `Step` struct:\\n\\n```rust\\n/// Sandbox mode for subprocess backends (FR-21).\\n/// Controls Codex `-s` and Gemini `--approval-mode`.\\n/// None = backend default (read-only).\\n#[serde(default)]\\npub sandbox: Option<SandboxMode>,\\n```\\n\\n**Import:** Add `use crate::backend::SandboxMode;` to the imports in `src/workflow.rs`.\\n\\n**Deserialization:** `SandboxMode` is defined in `src/backend/context.rs`. It needs `serde::Deserialize` and `serde::Serialize` derives with `#[serde(rename_all = \\\"kebab-case\\\")]` to parse `read-only`, `workspace-write`, `danger-full-access` from YAML. The file already imports serde types via `use serde_json::Value` but does not have `use serde::Deserialize;` — add `use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};`.\\n\\n**Current `SandboxMode` has no serde derives.** We need to add them:\\n\\n```rust\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Deserialize, Serialize)]\\n#[serde(rename_all = \\\"kebab-case\\\")]\\npub enum SandboxMode {\\n    ReadOnly,\\n    WorkspaceWrite,\\n    DangerFullAccess,\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### 2.2 `step_context()` — thread sandbox\\n\\n**File:** `src/workflow.rs` (line ~167)\\n\\n```rust\\nfn step_context<'a>(\\n    step: &'a Step,\\n    workflow: &Workflow,\\n    prompt: &'a str,\\n    cwd: &'a Path,\\n) -> backend::StepContext<'a> {\\n    backend::StepContext {\\n        sandbox: step.sandbox,\\n        timeout: workflow\\n            .step_timeout(step)\\n            .map(std::time::Duration::from_millis),\\n        ..backend::StepContext::from_prompt(prompt, cwd, step.model.as_deref())\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\nUpdate the doc comment to remove \\\"sandbox remains empty\\\" note.\\n\\n### 2.3 `CodexBackend` — dynamic sandbox arg injection\\n\\n**File:** `src/backend/codex.rs`\\n\\n**Change the `query` method** to build args dynamically based on `ctx.sandbox` instead of using `self.args` verbatim.\\n\\nKey logic:\\n\\n```rust\\nasync fn query(&self, ctx: StepContext<'_>) -> Result<QueryOutput, BackendError> {\\n    // ... existing setup ...\\n\\n    let mut cmd = Command::new(&self.command);\\n\\n    // Base args from config (may be empty -> use recommended defaults)\\n    if self.args.is_empty() {\\n        cmd.args([\\\"exec\\\", \\\"--json\\\", \\\"--ephemeral\\\"]);\\n    } else {\\n        cmd.args(&self.args);\\n    }\\n\\n    // Sandbox flag: ctx.sandbox overrides, fallback to read-only\\n    let sandbox = ctx.sandbox.unwrap_or(SandboxMode::ReadOnly);\\n    let sandbox_str = match sandbox {\\n        SandboxMode::ReadOnly => \\\"read-only\\\",\\n        SandboxMode::WorkspaceWrite => \\\"workspace-write\\\",\\n        SandboxMode::DangerFullAccess => \\\"danger-full-access\\\",\\n    };\\n    cmd.arg(\\\"-s\\\").arg(sandbox_str);\\n\\n    // Model override\\n    if let Some(m) = effective_model.as_ref() {\\n        cmd.arg(\\\"--model\\\").arg(m);\\n    }\\n\\n    // Prompt as positional arg\\n    cmd.arg(\\\"--\\\").arg(prompt)\\n        .current_dir(cwd)\\n        // ... rest unchanged ...\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**Design decisions:**\\n- Sandbox is injected AFTER base args so it overrides any `-s` in custom config args. This is intentional — per-step sandbox should take priority over backend config.\\n- `--ephemeral` is included ONLY in the no-custom-args default set. If the user configured custom args, we do NOT inject `--ephemeral` (preserving their explicit config).\\n- When custom `config.args` are provided, we still append sandbox at the end, preserving user-configured flags like `--ignore-user-config`.\\n\\n### 2.4 `GeminiBackend` — dynamic approval-mode injection\\n\\n**File:** `src/backend/gemini.rs`\\n\\nIn the shell command string construction, append `--approval-mode <mode>` based on `ctx.sandbox`:\\n\\n```rust\\nlet approval_flag = match ctx.sandbox {\\n    Some(SandboxMode::ReadOnly) => \\\" --approval-mode plan\\\",\\n    Some(SandboxMode::WorkspaceWrite) => \\\" --approval-mode auto_edit\\\",\\n    Some(SandboxMode::DangerFullAccess) => \\\" --approval-mode yolo\\\",\\n    None => \\\"\\\",  // backend default (no restriction)\\n};\\n```\\n\\n**Gemini approval mode mapping** (verified against `gemini-cli-gap-analysis.md` §5.8; final verification against `gemini --help` required at implementation time):\\n\\n| SandboxMode | `--approval-mode` | Effect |\\n|---|---|---|\\n| `ReadOnly` | `plan` | Read-only, no mutations |\\n| `WorkspaceWrite` | `auto_edit` | Auto-approve edit tools |\\n| `DangerFullAccess` | `yolo` | Auto-approve all (CLI only) |\\n| `None` | (not added) | Gemini default behaviour |\\n\\n**Design decision:** When `ctx.sandbox` is `None` (no per-step override), we add no `--approval-mode` flag. This differs from Codex where `None` falls back to `read-only`. Rationale: Gemini backends may be used for read-only tasks today without any flag; adding `--approval-mode plan` would be a behavioural change for all existing Gemini configurations. The v5 PRD treats `None` as \\\"backend default\\\" which for Gemini means the installed default (typically interactive).\\n\\n### 2.5 `SandboxMode` — add serde derives\\n\\n**File:** `src/backend/context.rs`\\n\\n```rust\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Deserialize, Serialize)]\\n#[serde(rename_all = \\\"kebab-case\\\")]\\npub enum SandboxMode {\\n    ReadOnly,\\n    WorkspaceWrite,\\n    DangerFullAccess,\\n}\\n```\\n\\nAlso update the `#[allow(dead_code)]` annotation — remove it once `Step.sandbox` starts consuming the enum.\\n\\n### 2.6 Other backends — no-op\\n\\nClaude, Ollama, and Bedrock backends do not use sandbox/approval-mode CLIs. No changes needed. The `ctx.sandbox` field is silently ignored.\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 3. The Problem Statement explicitly lists *\"Structured output requires a post-hoc extract_json_from_text call\"* as a broken behavior. However, a Constraint explicitly forbids moving `extract_json_from_text` out of `workflow.rs` and mandates a naive `serde_json::from_str`. Because LLMs almost always wrap JSON in markdown blocks (e.g., ````json {...} ````), `stdout.trim()` will fail to parse and `structured` will silently evaluate to `None`. This means the task will fail to solve the stated problem for the vast majority of real-world responses.\ndocs/reviews/clo-207-spec-review-gemini.md:42:1. **Resolve JSON Parsing Contradiction**: The naive `serde_json::from_str(stdout.trim())` will fail on markdown-fenced JSON, meaning `structured` will almost always be `None` in CLI/chat scenarios. Tables recurse; scalars/arrays replace.\nfn deep_merge(base: &mut toml::Value, overlay: toml::Value) {\n    match (base, overlay) {\n        (toml::Value::Table(base_table), toml::Value::Table(overlay_table)) => {\n            for (key, value) in overlay_table {\n                match base_table.get_mut(&key) {\n                    Some(existing) => deep_merge(existing, value),\n                    None => {\n                        base_table.insert(key, value);\n                    }\n                }\n            }\n        }\n        (base, overlay) => *base = overlay,\n    }\n}\n\n/// Merge a TOML file into a base value. Returns Ok(()) if file doesn't exist.\n/// Validates the file against Config struct first to catch unknown fields with\n/// file-specific error context before merging.\nfn merge_toml_file(base: &mut toml::Value, path: &Path) -> Result<()> {\n    let content = match fs::read_to_string(path) {\n        Ok(c) => c,\n        Err(e) if e.kind() == std::io::ErrorKind::NotFound => return Ok(()),\n        Err(e) => return Err(anyhow::anyhow!(\"Error reading {}: {}\", path.display(), e)),\n    };\n\n    // Validate against Config struct first to catch unknown fields with file context\n    let _: Config =\n        toml::from_str(&content).with_context(|| format!(\"Error parsing {}\", path.display()))?;\n\n    let overlay: toml::Value =\n        toml::from_str(&content).with_context(|| format!(\"Error parsing {}\", path.display()))?;\n\n    deep_merge(base, overlay);\n    Ok(())\n}\n\n/// Core config loading with injectable paths for testability.\npub fn load_config_from_paths(\n    cwd: &Path,\n base: toml::Value =\n        toml::Value::try_from(&default_config).context(\"Failed to serialize default config\")?;\n\n    // Explicit path: merge with defaults (not hollow)\n    if let Some(p) = explicit_path {\n        merge_toml_file(&mut base, p)?;\n        return base\n            .try_into::<Config>()\n            .with_context(|| format!(\"Error parsing {}\", p.display()));\n    }\n\n &user_config_path)?;\n    }\n\n    // Layer 3: project config (./lok.toml)\n    let project_config_path = cwd.join(\"lok.toml\");\n    merge_toml_file(&mut base, &project_config_path)?;\n\n    // Deserialize merged TOML into Config (deny_unknown_fields applied here)\n    base.try_into::<Config>()\n        .context(\"Failed to deserialize merged config\")\n}\n\npub fn load_config(path: Problem\\n\\nCodex sandbox mode (`-s read-only | workspace-write | danger-full-access`) and Gemini's `--approval-mode` are currently hardcoded into each backend's argv builder. The `StepContext.sandbox` field exists (from CLO-371) but is never populated. Without per-step sandbox:\\n\\n- `apply_edits` steps cannot use Codex because `-s read-only` blocks file writes\\n- Gemini has no `--approval-mode` support at all\\n- Users cannot control sandbox granularity per step\\n\\n**Out of scope:**\\n- FR-22 (default `workspace-write` for `apply_edits` steps with no explicit sandbox) — separate CLO\\n- FR-23 (per-step timeout) — already handled by `step.timeout` field\\n- FR-24/24a (per-step options, `include_directories`) — separate CLOs\\n- Claude/Ollama/Bedrock sandbox support — no-op, sandbox is meaningful only for CLI subprocess backends\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 2. Design\\n\\n### 2.1 `Step` struct — add `sandbox` field\\n\\n**File:** `src/workflow.rs`\\n\\nAdd to the `Step` struct:\\n\\n```rust\\n/// Sandbox mode for subprocess backends (FR-21).\\n/// Controls Codex `-s` and Gemini `--approval-mode`.\\n/// None = backend default (read-only).\\n#[serde(default)]\\npub sandbox: Option<SandboxMode>,\\n```\\n\\n**Import:** Add `use crate::backend::SandboxMode;` to the imports in `src/workflow.rs`.\\n\\n**Deserialization:** `SandboxMode` is defined in `src/backend/context.rs`. It needs `serde::Deserialize` and `serde::Serialize` derives with `#[serde(rename_all = \\\"kebab-case\\\")]` to parse `read-only`, `workspace-write`, `danger-full-access` from YAML. The file already imports serde types via `use serde_json::Value` but does not have `use serde::Deserialize;` — add `use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};`.\\n\\n**Current `SandboxMode` has no serde derives.** We need to add them:\\n\\n```rust\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Deserialize, Serialize)]\\n#[serde(rename_all = \\\"kebab-case\\\")]\\npub enum SandboxMode {\\n    ReadOnly,\\n    WorkspaceWrite,\\n    DangerFullAccess,\\n}\\n```\\n\\n### 2.2 `step_context()` — thread sandbox\\n\\n**File:** `src/workflow.rs` (line ~167)\\n\\n```rust\\nfn step_context<'a>(\\n    step: &'a Step,\\n    workflow: &Workflow,\\n    prompt: &'a str,\\n    cwd: &'a Path,\\n) -> backend::StepContext<'a> {\\n    backend::StepContext {\\n        sandbox: step.sandbox,\\n        timeout: workflow\\n            .step_timeout(step)\\n            .map(std::time::Duration::from_millis),\\n        ..backend::StepContext::from_prompt(prompt, cwd, step.model.as_deref())\\n    }\\n}\\n```\\n\\nUpdate the doc comment to remove \\\"sandbox remains empty\\\" note.\\n\\n### 2.3 `CodexBackend` — dynamic sandbox arg injection\\n\\n**File:** `src/backend/codex.rs`\\n\\n**Change the `query` method** to build args dynamically based on `ctx.sandbox` instead of using `self.args` verbatim.\\n\\nKey logic:\\n\\n```rust\\nasync fn query(&self, ctx: StepContext<'_>) -> Result<QueryOutput, BackendError> {\\n    // ... existing setup ...\\n\\n    let mut cmd = Command::new(&self.command);\\n\\n    // Base args from config (may be empty -> use recommended defaults)\\n    if self.args.is_empty() {\\n        cmd.args([\\\"exec\\\", \\\"--json\\\", \\\"--ephemeral\\\"]);\\n    } else {\\n        cmd.args(&self.args);\\n    }\\n\\n    // Sandbox flag: ctx.sandbox overrides, fallback to read-only\\n    let sandbox = ctx.sandbox.unwrap_or(SandboxMode::ReadOnly);\\n    let sandbox_str = match sandbox {\\n        SandboxMode::ReadOnly => \\\"read-only\\\",\\n        SandboxMode::WorkspaceWrite => \\\"workspace-write\\\",\\n        SandboxMode::DangerFullAccess => \\\"danger-full-access\\\",\\n    };\\n    cmd.arg(\\\"-s\\\").arg(sandbox_str);\\n\\n    // Model override\\n    if let Some(m) = effective_model.as_ref() {\\n        cmd.arg(\\\"--model\\\").arg(m);\\n    }\\n\\n    // Prompt as positional arg\\n    cmd.arg(\\\"--\\\").arg(prompt)\\n        .current_dir(cwd)\\n        // ... rest unchanged ...\\n}\\n```\\n\\n**Design decisions:**\\n- Sandbox is injected AFTER base args so it overrides any `-s` in custom config args. This is intentional — per-step sandbox should take priority over backend config.\\n- `--ephemeral` is included ONLY in the no-custom-args default set. If the user configured custom args, we do NOT inject `--ephemeral` (preserving their explicit config).\\n- When custom `config.args` are provided, we still append sandbox at the end, preserving user-configured flags like `--ignore-user-config`.\\n\\n### 2.4 `GeminiBackend` — dynamic approval-mode injection\\n\\n**File:** `src/backend/gemini.rs`\\n\\nIn the shell command string construction, append `--approval-mode <mode>` based on `ctx.sandbox`:\\n\\n```rust\\nlet approval_flag = match ctx.sandbox {\\n    Some(SandboxMode::ReadOnly) => \\\" --approval-mode plan\\\",\\n    Some(SandboxMode::WorkspaceWrite) => \\\" --approval-mode auto_edit\\\",\\n    Some(SandboxMode::DangerFullAccess) => \\\" --approval-mode yolo\\\",\\n    None => \\\"\\\",  // backend default (no restriction)\\n};\\n```\\n\\n**Gemini approval mode mapping** (verified against `gemini-cli-gap-analysis.md` §5.8; final verification against `gemini --help` required at implementation time):\\n\\n| SandboxMode | `--approval-mode` | Effect |\\n|---|---|---|\\n| `ReadOnly` | `plan` | Read-only, no mutations |\\n| `WorkspaceWrite` | `auto_edit` | Auto-approve edit tools |\\n| `DangerFullAccess` | `yolo` | Auto-approve all (CLI only) |\\n| `None` | (not added) | Gemini default behaviour |\\n\\n**Design decision:** When `ctx.sandbox` is `None` (no per-step override), we add no `--approval-mode` flag. This differs from Codex where `None` falls back to `read-only`. Rationale: Gemini backends may be used for read-only tasks today without any flag; adding `--approval-mode plan` would be a behavioural change for all existing Gemini configurations. The v5 PRD treats `None` as \\\"backend default\\\" which for Gemini means the installed default (typically interactive).\\n\\n### 2.5 `SandboxMode` — add serde derives\\n\\n**File:** `src/backend/context.rs`\\n\\n```rust\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Deserialize, Serialize)]\\n#[serde(rename_all = \\\"kebab-case\\\")]\\npub enum SandboxMode {\\n    ReadOnly,\\n    WorkspaceWrite,\\n    DangerFullAccess,\\n}\\n```\\n\\nAlso update the `#[allow(dead_code)]` annotation — remove it once `Step.sandbox` starts consuming the enum.\\n\\n### 2.6 Other backends — no-op\\n\\nClaude, Ollama, and Bedrock backends do not use sandbox/approval-mode CLIs. No changes needed. The `ctx.sandbox` field is silently ignored.\\n\\n---\\n\\n## 3. Implementation plan\\n\\n### 3.1 Files to change\\n\\n| File | Change | Lines |\\n|---|---|---|\\n| `src/backend/context.rs` | Add serde derives to `SandboxMode` | ~3 lines |\\n| `src/workflow.rs` | a real `Command`, use a test helper `MockBackend` (or a test-only struct with the same arg-building logic) that captures the intended argv as a `Vec<String>`.\\n\\n| Test | Assertion |\\n|---|---|\\n| `codex_sandbox_default` | `None` → Codex argv contains `-s read-only` |\\n| `codex_sandbox_workspace_write` | `Some(WorkspaceWrite)` → Codex argv contains `-s workspace-write` |\\n| `codex_sandbox_danger_full_access` | `Some(DangerFullAccess)` → Codex argv contains `-s danger-full-access` |\\n| `codex_defaults_include_ephemeral` | Default args include `--ephemeral` |\\n| `gemini_sandbox_default` | `None` → Gemini argv does NOT contain `--approval-mode` |\\n| `gemini_sandbox_read_only` | `Some(ReadOnly)` → Gemini argv contains `--approval-mode plan` |\\n| `gemini_sandbox_workspace_write` | `Some(WorkspaceWrite)` → Gemini argv contains `--approval-mode auto_edit` |\\n| `gemini_sandbox_danger` | `Some(DangerFullAccess)` → Gemini argv contains `--approval-mode yolo` |\\n| `step_yaml_parsing` | `sandbox: workspace-write` → `Step.sandbox == Some(WorkspaceWrite)` |\\n| `step_yaml_default` | No `sandbox` field → `Step.sandbox == None` |\\n\\n### 3.3 Risk assessment\\n\\n| Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation |\\n|---|---|---|---|\\n| Gemini approval-mode names differ from gap analysis | Medium | Low | Verify with `gemini --help` for Gemini | Low | Medium | The existing Gemini shell-cmd pattern already handles single-quote escaping; approval-mode is a simple append |\\n| `--ephemeral` breaks existing Codex behaviour | Low | Problem\\\\n\\\\nCodex sandbox mode (`-s read-only | workspace-write | danger-full-access`) and Gemini's `--approval-mode` are currently hardcoded into each backend's argv builder. The `StepContext.sandbox` field exists (from CLO-371) but is never populated. Without per-step sandbox:\\\\n\\\\n- `apply_edits` steps cannot use Codex because `-s read-only` blocks file writes\\\\n- Gemini has no `--approval-mode` support at all\\\\n- Users cannot control sandbox granularity per step\\\\n\\\\n**Out of scope:**\\\\n- FR-22 (default `workspace-write` for `apply_edits` steps with no explicit sandbox) — separate CLO\\\\n- FR-23 (per-step timeout) — already handled by `step.timeout` field\\\\n- FR-24/24a (per-step options, `include_directories`) — separate CLOs\\\\n- Claude/Ollama/Bedrock sandbox support — no-op, sandbox is meaningful only for CLI subprocess backends\\\\n\\\\n---\\\\n\\\\n## 2. Design\\\\n\\\\n### 2.1 `Step` struct — add `sandbox` field\\\\n\\\\n**File:** `src/workflow.rs`\\\\n\\\\nAdd to the `Step` struct:\\\\n\\\\n```rust\\\\n/// Sandbox mode for subprocess backends (FR-21).\\\\n/// Controls Codex `-s` and Gemini `--approval-mode`.\\\\n/// None = backend default (read-only).\\\\n#[serde(default)]\\\\npub sandbox: Option<SandboxMode>,\\\\n```\\\\n\\\\n**Import:** Add `use crate::backend::SandboxMode;` to the imports in `src/workflow.rs`.\\\\n\\\\n**Deserialization:** `SandboxMode` is defined in `src/backend/context.rs`. It needs `serde::Deserialize` and `serde::Serialize` derives with `#[serde(rename_all = \\\\\\\"kebab-case\\\\\\\")]` to parse `read-only`, `workspace-write`, `danger-full-access` from YAML. The file already imports serde types via `use serde_json::Value` but does not have `use serde::Deserialize;` — add `use serde::{Deserialize, Serialize};`.\\\\n\\\\n**Current `SandboxMode` has no serde derives.** We need to add them:\\\\n\\\\n```rust\\\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Deserialize, Serialize)]\\\\n#[serde(rename_all = \\\\\\\"kebab-case\\\\\\\")]\\\\npub enum SandboxMode {\\\\n    ReadOnly,\\\\n    WorkspaceWrite,\\\\n    DangerFullAccess,\\\\n}\\\\n```\\\\n\\\\n### 2.2 `step_context()` — thread sandbox\\\\n\\\\n**File:** `src/workflow.rs` (line ~167)\\\\n\\\\n```rust\\\\nfn step_context<'a>(\\\\n    step: &'a Step,\\\\n    workflow: &Workflow,\\\\n    prompt: &'a str,\\\\n    cwd: &'a Path,\\\\n) -> backend::StepContext<'a> {\\\\n    backend::StepContext {\\\\n        sandbox: step.sandbox,\\\\n        timeout: workflow\\\\n            .step_timeout(step)\\\\n            .map(std::time::Duration::from_millis),\\\\n        ..backend::StepContext::from_prompt(prompt, cwd, step.model.as_deref())\\\\n    }\\\\n}\\\\n```\\\\n\\\\nUpdate the doc comment to remove \\\\\\\"sandbox remains empty\\\\\\\" note.\\\\n\\\\n### 2.3 `CodexBackend` — dynamic sandbox arg injection\\\\n\\\\n**File:** `src/backend/codex.rs`\\\\n\\\\n**Change the `query` method** to build args dynamically based on `ctx.sandbox` instead of using `self.args` verbatim.\\\\n\\\\nKey logic:\\\\n\\\\n```rust\\\\nasync fn query(&self, ctx: StepContext<'_>) -> Result<QueryOutput, BackendError> {\\\\n    // ... existing setup ...\\\\n\\\\n    let mut cmd = Command::new(&self.command);\\\\n\\\\n    // Base args from config (may be empty -> use recommended defaults)\\\\n    if self.args.is_empty() {\\\\n        cmd.args([\\\\\\\"exec\\\\\\\", \\\\\\\"--json\\\\\\\", \\\\\\\"--ephemeral\\\\\\\"]);\\\\n    } else {\\\\n        cmd.args(&self.args);\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    // Sandbox flag: ctx.sandbox overrides, fallback to read-only\\\\n    let sandbox = ctx.sandbox.unwrap_or(SandboxMode::ReadOnly);\\\\n    let sandbox_str = match sandbox {\\\\n        SandboxMode::ReadOnly => \\\\\\\"read-only\\\\\\\",\\\\n        SandboxMode::WorkspaceWrite => \\\\\\\"workspace-write\\\\\\\",\\\\n        SandboxMode::DangerFullAccess => \\\\\\\"danger-full-access\\\\\\\",\\\\n    };\\\\n    cmd.arg(\\\\\\\"-s\\\\\\\").arg(sandbox_str);\\\\n\\\\n    // Model override\\\\n    if let Some(m) = effective_model.as_ref() {\\\\n        cmd.arg(\\\\\\\"--model\\\\\\\").arg(m);\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    // Prompt as positional arg\\\\n    cmd.arg(\\\\\\\"--\\\\\\\").arg(prompt)\\\\n        .current_dir(cwd)\\\\n        // ... rest unchanged ...\\\\n}\\\\n```\\\\n\\\\n**Design decisions:**\\\\n- Sandbox is injected AFTER base args so it overrides any `-s` in custom config args. This is intentional — per-step sandbox should take priority over backend config.\\\\n- `--ephemeral` is included ONLY in the no-custom-args default set. If the user configured custom args, we do NOT inject `--ephemeral` (preserving their explicit config).\\\\n- When custom `config.args` are provided, we still append sandbox at the end, preserving user-configured flags like `--ignore-user-config`.\\\\n\\\\n### 2.4 `GeminiBackend` — dynamic approval-mode injection\\\\n\\\\n**File:** `src/backend/gemini.rs`\\\\n\\\\nIn the shell command string construction, append `--approval-mode <mode>` based on `ctx.sandbox`:\\\\n\\\\n```rust\\\\nlet approval_flag = match ctx.sandbox {\\\\n    Some(SandboxMode::ReadOnly) => \\\\\\\" --approval-mode plan\\\\\\\",\\\\n    Some(SandboxMode::WorkspaceWrite) => \\\\\\\" --approval-mode auto_edit\\\\\\\",\\\\n    Some(SandboxMode::DangerFullAccess) => \\\\\\\" --approval-mode yolo\\\\\\\",\\\\n    None => \\\\\\\"\\\\\\\",  // backend default (no restriction)\\\\n};\\\\n```\\\\n\\\\n**Gemini approval mode mapping** (verified against `gemini-cli-gap-analysis.md` §5.8; final verification against `gemini --help` required at implementation time):\\\\n\\\\n| SandboxMode | `--approval-mode` | Effect |\\\\n|---|---|---|\\\\n| `ReadOnly` | `plan` | Read-only, no mutations |\\\\n| `WorkspaceWrite` | `auto_edit` | Auto-approve edit tools |\\\\n| `DangerFullAccess` | `yolo` | Auto-approve all (CLI only) |\\\\n| `None` | (not added) | Gemini default behaviour |\\\\n\\\\n**Design decision:** When `ctx.sandbox` is `None` (no per-step override), we add no `--approval-mode` flag. This differs from Codex where `None` falls back to `read-only`. Rationale: Gemini backends may be used for read-only tasks today without any flag; adding `--approval-mode plan` would be a behavioural change for all existing Gemini configurations. The v5 PRD treats `None` as \\\\\\\"backend default\\\\\\\" which for Gemini means the installed default (typically interactive).\\\\n\\\\n### 2.5 `SandboxMode` — add serde derives\\\\n\\\\n**File:** `src/backend/context.rs`\\\\n\\\\n```rust\\\\n#[derive(Debug, Clone, Copy, PartialEq, Eq, Deserialize, Serialize)]\\\\n#[serde(rename_all = \\\\\\\"kebab-case\\\\\\\")]\\\\npub enum SandboxMode {\\\\n    ReadOnly,\\\\n    WorkspaceWrite,\\\\n    DangerFullAccess,\\\\n}\\\\n```\\\\n\\\\nAlso update the `#[allow(dead_code)]` annotation — remove it once `Step.sandbox` starts consuming the enum.\\\\n\\\\n### 2.6 Other backends — no-op\\\\n\\\\nClaude, Ollama, and Bedrock backends do not use sandbox/approval-mode CLIs. No changes needed. The `ctx.sandbox` field is silently ignored.\\\\n\\\\n---\\\\n\\\\n## 3. Implementation plan\\\\n\\\\n### 3.1 Files to change\\\\n\\\\n| File | Change | Lines |\\\\n|---|---|---|\\\\n| `src/backend/context.rs` | Add serde derives to `SandboxMode` | ~3 lines |\\\\n| building**\\\\n\\\\nSince we cannot easily capture process argv from a real `Command`, use a test helper `MockBackend` (or a test-only struct with the same arg-building logic) that captures the intended argv as a `Vec<String>`.\\\\n\\\\n| Test | Assertion |\\\\n|---|---|\\\\n| `codex_sandbox_default` | `None` → Codex argv contains `-s read-only` |\\\\n| `codex_sandbox_workspace_write` | `Some(WorkspaceWrite)` → Codex argv contains `-s workspace-write` |\\\\n| `codex_sandbox_danger_full_access` | `Some(DangerFullAccess)` → Codex argv contains `-s danger-full-access` |\\\\n| `codex_defaults_include_ephemeral` | Default args include `--ephemeral` |\\\\n| `gemini_sandbox_default` | `None` → Gemini argv does NOT contain `--approval-mode` |\\\\n| `gemini_sandbox_read_only` | `Some(ReadOnly)` → Gemini argv contains `--approval-mode plan` |\\\\n| `gemini_sandbox_workspace_write` | `Some(WorkspaceWrite)` → Gemini argv contains `--approval-mode auto_edit` |\\\\n| `gemini_sandbox_danger` | `Some(DangerFullAccess)` → Gemini argv contains `--approval-mode yolo` |\\\\n| `step_yaml_parsing` | `sandbox: workspace-write` → `Step.sandbox == Some(WorkspaceWrite)` |\\\\n| `step_yaml_default` | No `sandbox` field → `Step.sandbox == None` |\\\\n\\\\n### 3.3 Risk assessment\\\\n\\\\n| Risk | Likelihood | Impact | Mitigation |\\\\n|---|---|---|---|\\\\n| Gemini approval-mode names differ from gap analysis | Medium | Low | Verify with `gemini --help` at implementation time |\\\\n| Codex custom config args contain `-s` already | Low | Medium | Sandbox is appended after base args; per-step wins over config |\\\\n| Shell command string escaping breaks for Gemini | Low | Medium | The existing Gemini shell-cmd pattern already handles single-quote escaping; approval-mode is a simple append |\\\\n| `--ephemeral` breaks existing Codex behaviour | Low | Low | Per codex-quick-ref.md, this is a recommended addition; it only suppresses session artifact persistence |\\\\n\\\\n---\\\\n\\\\n## 4. Acceptance criteria\\\\n\\\\n- [ ] `SandboxMode` has serde derives with `rename_all = \\\\\\\"kebab-case\\\\\\\"` parsing `read-only`, `workspace-write`, `danger-full-access`\\\\n- [ ] `Step` struct has `sandbox: Option<SandboxMode>` field with `#[serde(rename = \\\\\\\"sandbox\\\\\\\")]`\\\\n- [ ] `step_context()` in `src/workflow.rs` threads `step.sandbox` into `StepContext.sandbox`\\\\n- [ ] `CodexBackend::query` uses `ctx.sandbox` to inject `-s <mode>`; `None` → `read-only`\\\\n- [ ] `GeminiBackend::query` uses `ctx.sandbox` to inject `--approval-mode <mode>`; `None` → no flag\\\\n- [ ] Default Codex args include `--ephemeral` (per codex-quick-ref.md recommended defaults)\\\\n- [ ] `cargo test` passes with argv-capture tests for all sandbox levels\\\\n- [ ] `cargo clippy -- -D warnings` clean\\\\n- [ ] Gemini approval-mode names verified against `gemini --help` and documented in PR description\\\\n\\\\n---\\\\n\\\\n## 5. .unwrap_or_default();\\\\n\\\\n        // Approval mode: per-step ctx.sandbox controls --approval-mode\\\\n        // None = no flag (Gemini default behaviour retained)\\\\n        let approval_flag = \\\\\\\"gemini\\\\\\\",\\\\n            start.elapsed(),\\\\n        )\\\\n        .with_model(effective_model))\\\\n    }\\\\n\\\\n    fn is_available(&self) -> bool {\\\\n
